Fengshan Road Under Japanese Control 75

Tianjin Correspondence: Since the fall of Jinzhou, all of our troops have retreated into Shanhaiguan. All land and political power outside the customs has been occupied by the Japanese. The Guandong section of the Beining Railway accounts for three-quarters of the entire line, including the Datong branch line, Gouying branch line, Jinzhou branch line, and Yingkou Wharf and Huludao Port, which the Japanese have long coveted. Now that they have occupied it by force, they are vigorously managing it. The puppet Fengtian Provincial Government has appointed Kan Duo as the director of the Guandong section and renamed the Guandong section of the Beining Railway the Fengshan Railway. At the same time, the six million yuan in cash that the former Beining Railway had stored in Shenyang (this money was for the development of Huludao Port and construction of a harbor, but it was seized by the Japanese after the September 18th Incident) has been withdrawn to be used to buy off our Chinese employees at various stations. Now Kan Duo has established a temporary office of the Fengshan Railway in the Transportation Bank building at the Japanese station and is carrying out official business. On the other hand, a large number of personnel have been dispatched along the line, claiming that employees of the Guandong section who have left their posts will be paid three months' salary in advance as an incentive if they report to the office before the 19th. Those who do not report after the deadline will be dismissed. The announcement issued by Kan Duo is copied below: "I have been appointed by the Fengtian Provincial Government as the Director of the Fengshan Railway Administration. I have taken office today. Since the incident, the officials of this railway have maintained it with great effort. Recently, due to military relations, many have left their posts, resulting in a standstill in transportation and business. The Director of this Bureau is tasked with handling all affairs of the entire railway, with the primary goal of restoring the original state. All original employees and workers in all parts of this railway must be at ease and continue to serve as usual. Those who have temporarily left their posts must return to their original posts within ten days and report to the Bureau. Those who do not report after the deadline will be dismissed without leniency. You must obey. Director Kan Duo, January 9th."

After the Riot by Japanese in Qingdao 76

The Municipal Party Department Has Dissolved Itself

Publication of the Minguo Daily Postponed Indefinitely

Qingdao Correspondence: Since the municipal party headquarters was burned down by Japanese rioters, all the luggage and clothing of the staff of the party headquarters were not able to be taken out at the time and have been turned to ashes. Only the staff members themselves escaped and are temporarily staying in various hotels, their situation is extremely embarrassing. Yesterday (the 16th), the executive committee members of the municipal party headquarters held a meeting in the library on Juxian Road to discuss the aftermath. It was resolved that: 1. All work of the municipal party headquarters will be suspended until further orders from the Central Government. 2. Each staff member of the party headquarters will first be paid two months' salary as a relief fund, and the party headquarters will be temporarily dissolved pending a recall order. 3. Publication of the Minguo Daily has been temporarily suspended due to excessive losses, and the date of resumption of publication will be determined later. The staff and workers of the newspaper will be paid one and a half months' salary and dismissed. 4. The National News Agency will also be temporarily suspended and the staff will be paid two months' salary. After the above measures were decided, the salaries were paid out today and the municipal party headquarters has been dissolved. As for the executive and supervisory committee members, they will await orders from the Central Government before making a decision.

Also, it has been widely rumored in the city recently that the Japanese person, Doihara, secretly came to Qingdao a few days ago and will carry out further activities. The citizens talk about it with great fear, and the people are quite uneasy these days. The Japanese expatriates are also scheduled to hold a meeting of expatriates at the residential group tomorrow, and it is feared that there will be another conspiracy. Because of the Japanese burning down the municipal party headquarters, the municipal government has lodged a serious protest with the Japanese consul in Qingdao. After three days, the Japanese consul has not yet replied. It is reported that the municipal government will file a second protest (January 17th).

Shandong Audit Office Still Belongs to the Central Government 77

Result of Belsons' Negotiations in Jinan

Jinan Correspondence: After Han Fuju took over the national tax agencies, he sent Li Wuchen to act as the Shandong Salt Transport Department Tax Police, which was taken over from the audit office. Jiao Zilong was appointed as the team leader and Chai Dongsheng was appointed as the manager of the Shandong Salt Affairs Audit Branch and went to take over. The manager of the office, Li Zhifan, immediately handed over the office to the deputy manager, an Englishman, Buske, who raised an objection due to the loan contract relationship and telegraphed the Salt Affairs Audit General Office to request instructions. The general office then sent the former director of the Shandong Audit Office, an Englishman, Belson, and special commissioner Zeng Yangfeng to Jinan to negotiate with Han Fuju at the provincial government on the 18th. Belson explained the purpose of his visit and said that the government also understood Shandong's financial difficulties very well, but the audit office, customs, and postal service have always been managed uniformly by the central government, and the system should not be disrupted. The audit office has achieved remarkable results. The salt tax in the early years was only 20 million yuan, but last year it has increased to 160 million yuan, which is of great importance to the central government's finances. If it is transferred to the jurisdiction of the provincial government, tax revenue may be affected, and Shandong should not be different from the rest of the country. The tax police were not originally managed by the audit office, but after the audit office took over due to rampant corruption, there has been some improvement, and it is hoped that they will still be managed by the audit office. As for the tax funds, after deducting foreign debts and the expenses of the audit office, the remaining funds will be temporarily left in Shandong to replenish military expenditures, and the original situation will be restored after the central government funds can be issued. In this way, both the central administrative system and the local difficulties in Shandong can be taken into account. Otherwise, if this precedent is set, other places may follow suit. Han said that he has always supported unification, and this time the borrowing of central tax funds was a last resort. After the central government funds arrive and military expenditures can be issued, the national tax agencies will be immediately returned. The audit office can still order the former director Li Zhifan to be reinstated, and Chai Dongsheng will be appointed as the team leader of the tax police brigade, which will still be under the jurisdiction of the audit office. The tax funds (i.e., surplus salt revenue) will be temporarily borrowed. This negotiation was then resolved. Belson, Zeng Yangfeng, and others are scheduled to go to Yantai in the coming days. It is reported that the Yantai tax police can also still be managed by the audit office (January 19th).

8,000-Year-Old Zhang Heilian and Other Units Also Surrender

Dispute Between Hebei Anti-Drug Association and Party Department 79

Provincial Party Department Bans the Work of the Anti-Drug Association

Tianjin Correspondence: The northern part of Hebei Province borders Rehe, and the southern part borders Henan, both of which are opium producing areas. In addition, there are many local opium dealers in this province, so opium is extremely prevalent. Last year, the China National Anti-Drug Association entrusted Cao Hongzhu to come to Tianjin to advocate the establishment of the Hebei Provincial National Anti-Drug Branch to seek the eradication of opium. All circles unanimously agreed and elected Cao Hongzhu, Zhou Zhaoxiang, Wang Wendian, Leng Jiaji, Zhang Zhongyuan, Sun Fengzao, Zhu Qinghua, Wu Chengshi, Wu Aichen, Chen Mingjian, Liu Mengyang, Li Quan, Gao Xingya, Su Rongquan, Li Jinghu, and Chen Xisan as committee members, and Cao Hongzhu as chairman. The organization was legally established in May and was issued a certificate by the Tianjin Municipal Party Department and approved and filed by the Provincial Government. It was formally established on June 24. At that time, the Provincial Party Department specially sent Wang Renmin to attend the swearing-in ceremony, so the organization of the association was sound in accordance with the organizational plan. In the past six months, in addition to carrying out propaganda, investigation, and reporting, it has also strived to advocate anti-drug activities in accordance with the organizational outline of the General Association and has successively obtained the initiation of the organization of county branches in various counties to cooperate with the provincial branch to eradicate the drug disaster. However, the opium disaster in Hebei is rampant and its momentum is overwhelming. Although the provincial government has strictly prohibited it and issued strict orders, some corrupt officials have colluded to make a profit. Not only do they turn a deaf ear to the provincial orders, but they even regard the anti-drug associations of the public as hindering their actions and use all kinds of threats and obstacles. Therefore, on December 28, 20th year, the provincial government ordered all cities and counties to effectively assist the Hebei Provincial Anti-Drug Branch. Unexpectedly, just as the letters were being distributed, the Hebei Provincial Party Department issued a notice to the party departments of various counties, saying that the Hebei Provincial Anti-Drug Branch had not been approved to organize at all. How could it organize county branches in various counties? It was ordered to be banned, etc. The provincial branch, when the organization was first established, had reported to the party and government organs in the location for guidance and filing. The opening of the meeting also had representatives of the party department present to participate. How could the facts be erased and arbitrarily destroyed? Moreover, the party department should be in a guiding position. How can it oppress public opinion and forcibly stop the assembly? People have absolute freedom in law, as stipulated in the provisional constitution. How can it be destroyed? The provincial party department does not understand its position and abuses its power, which not only violates Sun Yat-sen's advocacy of civil rights, but also borders on autocratic behavior. Moreover, when the country is in trouble, anti-drug is the foundation of strengthening the people. All Chinese citizens should work together to save the country from ruin. Therefore, the association has replied to the provincial party department with a letter based on the above reasons and telegraphed the Nanjing Central Party Department, asking it to quickly stop the actions of the provincial party department in order to maintain the ban on opium (January 17th).

Partial Exemption of Grain Tribute and Additional Levies: The Ministry of Finance had previously approved a one-year extension for the additional levy of two yuan per stone of grain tribute. The case of Jiangsu Province's application for a one-year extension of the additional grain levy had been repeatedly submitted to the Executive Yuan's Secretariat in April of the 20th year, which forwarded it to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, requesting that the two yuan additional grain levy from the 19th year be extended for one year within the 20th-year budget. This ministry had separately listed the reasons for not approving the extension and requested that the original plan be maintained. Subsequently, a letter was received from the Executive Yuan's Secretariat, forwarded to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, again requesting a one-year extension of the two yuan additional grain levy. Furthermore, since this case had been repeatedly submitted by the Jiangsu Provincial Government and is now during the period of bandit suppression, it seems feasible to proceed accordingly. However, Jiangsu Province's land tax is notoriously heavy, with additional levies on top of the regular tax. During this one-year extension period, each county must not add any additional levies under the land tax item. After the expiration of the period, the provincial government must not request a renewal under any pretext." This ministry has ordered the Jiangsu Department of Finance to comply with the above, which should be noted.

Jiangyin 84

Headquarters Interrogates Robbers of Dada Steamer: The Dada Steamer of the Shanghai-Yangzhou route was robbed in the Jiangmian waters of Liuwei Port in November of last year, resulting in significant losses. After investigations by Huang Bingzhong, the captain of the Detective Team of the Suchang Pacification Headquarters, it was discovered that Yan Linlin, a key suspect in the case, from Weitang, Changzhou, had partnered with others to rob the Dada Steamer. He had since been appointed as a patrol ship cabin chief in the 8th Anti-Smuggling Brigade of Suzhou. He was immediately arrested and brought to the headquarters. On the 18th, after being questioned by Chief Zhu, he was transferred to the County Government for detention. Another suspect, Geng, is scheduled to be brought to the headquarters for interrogation on the 19th.

Ministry of Communications' Ban on Private Postal Bureaus: The Ministry of Communications ordered that all private postal bureaus be shut down by the end of the 20th year. The Jiangyin Quansheng and other postal bureaus had submitted a request to the Chamber of Commerce to forward to the Ministry of Communications, requesting an extension of the closure period for ten years. The Ministry of Communications replied that the postal service is a state-run enterprise, and the ministry has already been lenient in allowing private postal bureaus to operate with registered licenses. The submission states that the general delivery of letters to the post office is slow, and merchants and the public must send them through private bureaus, leaving the private bureaus without business. This is a misunderstanding. The temporary regulations for private bureaus' registered licenses stipulate that if a location from which or to which a letter is sent does not have a post office or a postal kiosk, or another village or town postal delivery service, the private bureau is still allowed to deliver the letter themselves. It is not required that all letters be delivered to the post office for general delivery. Therefore, the ministry has already considered both the operation and the livelihood of the merchants and the public. If the private bureaus register with the post office, they can continue to operate within the aforementioned scope. There is no need to discuss the request for a ten-year extension.

Principals in Attendance 88

The principals in attendance included Li Weizhang (Huai'an Agricultural), Ren Zhongmin (Zhenjiang Middle), Sun Ting sheng (Nanjing Middle), Zheng Tonghe (Shanghai Middle), Shen Zhensheng (Ru Middle), Chen Lun (Wuxi Middle), Tao Xuan (Beijing Women's Middle), Hu Huanyong (Suzhou Middle), Gu Zhonghua (Taicang Middle), Zheng Bijiang (Women's A), Peng Daquan (Yancheng Middle), Zhou Hou shu (Yangzhou Middle), Wang Delin (Huaiyin Middle), Sun Jiehuang (Donghai Middle), Zhu (Changzhou Middle), Xue Zhongtai (Xuzhou Middle), Jiang Xuezhu (Songjiang Women's Middle), Yu Yu (Xuzhou Women's Middle), Wang Maozu (Beijing Middle), Zhang Jinan (Suqian Middle), Chen Shu (Suzhou Women's Middle), Chen Shi (Huai'an Middle), Chen Jing (Songjiang Middle), and Zhang Haicheng (Nantong Middle), totaling twenty-two people.

Zhou Fohai's Report 89

After Zhou Fohai, the chairman, performed the formalities, Zhou made a brief report, stating that his coming to Jiangsu to lead education was somewhat forced, especially as he was not very familiar with the situation in Jiangsu. Therefore, it was necessary to meet with everyone to discuss everything. The Education Department is currently preparing several discussion topics to exchange opinions. Since everyone has met with Chairman Gu, they also feel that funding is a difficult issue. He is willing to be everyone's vanguard regarding funding, and will not be deterred by any difficulties. He also hopes that everyone will work together, etc.

Section Chief Hou's Report 90

Next, Section Chief Hou reported: ㈠ Regarding the submission to the Central Government for additional funding for National Central University: It has been found that the educational funding in this province is extremely strained and must be remedied urgently. It was previously submitted to the 463rd meeting of the Provincial Government Committee, which resolved to transfer the cigarette tax in Jiangsu Province to the Ministry of Finance and Education for the funding of National Central University, and that all income from the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office from January 21st onwards would be used to supplement the Provincial Education Funding for maintenance, etc. This was also submitted separately to the Provincial Government. It was previously reported that the Executive Yuan's meeting on January 12th resolved that the Central University's maintenance funding of 1.32 million would be permanently provided by the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office. This was discussed at the 27th Education Funding Committee meeting on January 13th. It was resolved that the Provincial Government should continue to strongly advocate to the Central Government and that, as both Central University and Provincial Education funding are facing difficulties, they should jointly request relief from the Executive Yuan and discuss the solution after the results are obtained. ㈡ Regarding the relief of the current financial difficulties of provincial education in order to maintain operations: It has been found that this year's provincial educational funding has been severely impacted by the famine, and all agencies have been in arrears with their regular expenses for several months, facing extreme hardship. If relief is not sought quickly, operations will be suspended. The 27th Education Funding Committee previously resolved to maintain provincial educational funding before December of the 20th year, awaiting the return of the Director of the Finance Department to the province to discuss whether to temporarily borrow and pledge securities or temporarily transfer other funds for relief, etc. The department is currently working with the management office to find ways to provide urgent relief. As for the shortfall in revenue and expenditure for the entire year, including previous accumulated losses, the management office reports that it amounts to 2.4 million yuan. How to seek relief will be proposed for discussion at the next Education Funding Committee meeting. ㈢ Regarding the examination and selection of current employees of provincial educational institutions to study abroad: In order to increase the efficiency of educational services, the department submitted a proposal to the 464th meeting of the Provincial Government Committee, which resolved to examine and select current employees of provincial educational institutions to study abroad from the 21st year onwards. The department is currently preparing a detailed plan for implementation.

The items for discussion today include four: ㈠ Studying the implementation of moral education policies in order to rectify the academic atmosphere and eliminate student unrest; ㈡ Studying the implementation of the Ministry-promulgated junior and senior high school curriculum standards; ㈢ Studying how vocational education should be promoted and improved; ㈣ Studying how normal school education should be improved.

Zheng Xigu's Speech 91

Zheng Xigu, the principal of Shanghai Middle School, stated that since the director has taken office, there has been a very good phenomenon of rapid progress in Jiangsu education. He feels very fortunate to be able to gather with the director today to discuss matters. He hopes that ㈠ the department will consider the opinions of each school in its plans; ㈡ the department will support each school in complying with and carrying out its plans; ㈢ he requests that the department provide a practical discussion today regarding the issues of rectifying the academic atmosphere, normal school independence, and resolving financial difficulties.

Discussion of Various Matters 92

㈠ Regarding the financial issue, Zhang Haicheng first reported on the situation of stating to Sun Ke, the President of the Executive Yuan, that the Executive Yuan could no longer order the change of law to have Jiangsu permanently bear the expenses of Central University. Sun agreed that the government would never issue illegal orders. He also asked the Ministry of Education to submit a reconsideration to the Executive Yuan to cancel the previous resolution that the expenses of Central University would be permanently allocated from Jiangsu. He hopes that the department will ask the provincial government to realize the resolution. Next, Zhou Fohai said that he would do his best to address the financial problem, no matter how much Central University opposes it, Jiangsu must maintain the implementation of the resolution, and if necessary, he will propose a remedy at the provincial government, which will be used for education and not for raising soldiers.

㈡ Studying the implementation of moral education policies in order to rectify the academic atmosphere and eliminate student unrest, Director Zhou started by saying that the motivation for proposing this case is that education is currently too unstable. If we do not start with rectifying the academic atmosphere, education is equivalent to nothing. His personal opinion is to proceed from three points: (1) He plans to go to Beijing, Shanghai, and various counties in Jiangbei in early February to give practical lectures to students on the path they should take in the future. (2) He asks the faculty and staff of each school to assist the principal in participating in student groups to lead students to work together. (3) Hold a lecture every week to study the Northeast issue in Japan.

Next, President Ren of Zhenjiang Middle School, President of Shanghai Middle School, President Zhou of Middle School, President Tao of Beijing Women's Middle School, President Zhang of Nanjing Middle School, and the academics presented their views. The main points: (1) Central politics must be on track, and the student unrest in national universities must be eliminated first; (2) The Education Department must assist middle school principals in dealing with student unrest; (3) The Party Department must have a unified method for student organizations; (4) The student self-government association cannot exceed the school's management; (5) In addition to Party doctrine, civic education must be compulsory; (6) Each subject must be centered on the Three Principles of the People, and there is no need to make the Three Principles of the People a separate subject, which would make students feel pointless due to the lack of competent teachers; (7) Faculty and staff must participate in students' national salvation movement and fulfill their responsibilities of protection, guidance, and restraint.

This case was concluded without taking a resolution. The above points will be the standard for future moral education and are expected to be gradually implemented. The meeting was adjourned at 12 noon, and the meeting continued after lunch.

The meeting resumed at 2 p.m. to continue discussing the proposals submitted by the Education Department, and the results are as follows:

㈢ Implementing the Ministry-promulgated junior and senior high school curriculum standards: 1. Organize a provincial education design committee; 2. The department will collect the Ministry of Education's proposed revisions to the curriculum standards and distribute them to each school for study, solicit opinions, and organize a committee to discuss and decide.

㈣ Studying how vocational education should be promoted and improved: 1. The Education Department will convene experts and representatives of middle school principals to comprehensively plan and implement.

㈤ How to improve normal school education: 1. Expand rural teachers' schools and grant them independence; 2. Gradually restrict senior high school normal courses and select locations to establish several independent schools; 3. Starting from the new students enrolled in the 21st year, normal school students must practice elementary school education for one year after completing their studies before being awarded a graduation certificate. During the internship period, the elementary school will provide food, accommodation, and travel expenses, and may give a discretionary allowance; 4. Increase the salaries of qualified elementary school teachers; 5. Promulgate an order to protect the services of qualified elementary school teachers.

㈥ The following provisional motions were resolved: (1) Starting from the 21st year, principals will be sent abroad in batches for observation; (2) The Education Department will convene principals to solicit opinions when discussing the budget for the 21st year; (3) The Funding Management Office must relocate to Zhenjiang within this year; (4) Supplementary distribution of the remaining funds from the 18th year and the temporary expenses from the 20th year; (5) Convene a meeting of principals twice per semester; (6) Please clearly specify the disaster areas that must be free of charge and clarify that the exempted miscellaneous fees and graduate accommodation fees must be deducted from the total accommodation fees. Please specify another allocation to compensate for those who do not have accommodation fees;

(7) The Education Department will immediately request the provincial schools to provide relief to the elementary school teachers in the disaster areas of this province and distribute the relief funds to the teachers as soon as possible to provide relief.

Famous Heavenly Calculation Expert Wang Xi'en Passes Away 94

Jinan Correspondence: Wang Xi'en, the chairman of the Department of Heavenly Calculation at Qilu University in Jinan, was a world-renowned expert in heavenly calculation. He had studied heavenly calculation for more than forty years, and his depth of knowledge was rare in China. His published works include more than ten kinds such as Practical Astronomy, Gougu Yandai Illustrated Explanation, Trigonometry, Physical Calculus, Radio Science, Radio Science Principles, etc. His recent invention of a new algorithm for graphically calculating solar eclipses has been spread throughout Europe and America, and has been highly regarded by heavenly calculation experts in various countries. Astronomical journals from various countries have competed to publish his works, and his name has become widely known in Europe and America. The Paris World Astronomical Society has sent a special letter inviting him to join the society (the members of the society are all world-renowned heavenly calculation experts). He passed away on the morning of January 13th due to overwork. All those who had heard of his name were shocked and grieved by this sad news. The sudden passing of such a mentor in the scientific community is not only a misfortune for one school or one country, but for the world. It is reported that the school, in order to honor the senior, will suspend classes and lower the flag to half-mast on the day of his funeral (January 23rd) to show their condolences.

Selection of the Hong Kong Team for the Inter-Port Football Match 105

Chinese Have Not Participated

A Brief History of the Inter-Port Competition 106

The inter-port football competition originated in 1908 with matches between Western teams from Shanghai and Hong Kong. The competition was suspended for ten years due to the outbreak of the European War in 1913. In 1913, the Shanghai Western team defeated the Hong Kong team 2-1 in overtime. The official inter-port competition began in 1923 with the Hong Kong Telegraph Cup. Hankou joined the following year, and the Shanghai-Hong Kong final ended in a draw. Shanghai won the replay 1-0 and took the silver cup. Hong Kong won the following year, and the two teams took turns winning until Shanghai won two consecutive years starting the year before last. In total, Shanghai has won seven times and Hong Kong four times.

Hong Kong Team Lineup 107

Since the separation of the Chinese and Hong Kong clubs in Hong Kong this year, no Chinese players will participate in this trip to Shanghai. The entire team of fourteen players will be selected from the following four teams: Civilians (winner of this year's Li Hua Cup), Hong Kong Football Club (H.F.C.), Kowloon Club, and Borders. The approximate lineup is as follows:

Chinese Youth Association Basketball Tournament 110

Registration Starts Today

The football league organized by the Chinese Youth Association on Sichuan Road has entered its fourth week, so the association is now engaged in holding a basketball league. It is heard that registration will begin today. The regulations are recorded below:

Chinese Youth Basketball League Regulations

㈠ Name: Second Chinese Youth Basketball League ㈡ Purpose: To promote basketball games, enhance competition experience and skills. ㈢ Qualifications: Anyone who is not employed in sports can organize a team to participate. ㈣ Registration: From the 21st to the 31st of this month, registration will close when the quota is full. ㈤ Registration Procedures: 1. Submit a 6-inch photo of all team members (those without photos will not be registered). 2. List of team members (those participating in the Chinese Sports Association and Western Youth Association leagues will not be registered). 3. Pay the fees due. ㈥ Fees: 1. Registration fee 2. Guarantee deposit of 5 yuan. ㈦ Quota: 60 teams, divided into six groups: "Zhong", "Qing", "Lan", "Qiu", "Lian", "Sai". ㈧ Competition Time: Each game will last 32 minutes, with a 5-minute rest period in between. A team that is more than 5 minutes late will be considered to have forfeited. If neither team appears, both teams will be considered to have forfeited. Any team that forfeits twice will lose its eligibility to compete. ㈨ Competition Location: Basketball court of this association on Sichuan Road. ㈩ Postponement: Any team that needs to postpone a game due to unavoidable circumstances must obtain permission from this association two days before the game. ㈩㈠ Uniforms: Teams without uniforms and players without numbers will not be allowed to participate in the competition. ㈩㈡ Membership Card: Each team will be issued a maximum of 12 membership cards, which are only valid for that team's own games. ㈩㈢ Awards: 1. The champion of each group will be awarded a silver shield. 2. The overall championship will be inscribed on the large silver cup specially prepared by this association. ㈩㈣ Penalties: 1. Any team that violates Article 5, Section 2 of these regulations will have its trophy withheld and its guarantee deposit cancelled. 2. Any team that forfeits once will have half of its guarantee deposit deducted. Any team that forfeits twice will be considered to have withdrawn from the competition. 3. Any team that withdraws from the competition midway will have its guarantee deposit confiscated. ㈩㈤ Protests: If unfortunately a protest occurs, it must be submitted in writing to the committee of this association within two days of the event, and a guarantee deposit of 5 yuan must be paid at the same time. If the committee believes that the protest is well-founded, the guarantee deposit will be refunded; otherwise, it will be confiscated. However, the committee's decision is final and cannot be appealed. ㈩㈥ This association has established a special committee to handle all matters. ㈩㈦ The committee of this association may amend these regulations at any time if there are any deficiencies.

Page 11

Free Talk

Right and Wrong (Part 1) 112

Mencius said, "The heart of right and wrong is possessed by all men." Physiologists and psychologists have dissected and experimented on the human brain thousands of times, but have yet to find a specific area responsible for right and wrong.

Right and wrong are merely symbols used to judge behavior. The ability to make these judgments is acquired through experience. It is a skill learned in practical life, not an innate sense of morality or ability.

In practical life, people assign a certain symbol to a certain behavior without any ambiguity. Over time, it becomes second nature. What is right will be called right, and what is wrong will be called wrong, without any discrepancy. If, in practical life, someone confuses black and white, calls a deer a horse, sometimes calling what is right wrong and what is wrong right, then right and wrong cannot be clearly distinguished.

Why should right and wrong be reversed? Generally, when seeking personal gain, people do not want right and wrong to be clear. Only when they suffer a slight loss do they loudly demand that others distinguish between right and wrong. "Right and wrong" is the enemy of those who seek advantage. "Knowing right and wrong" is the call for help from those who suffer losses. People cannot always seek advantage, nor can they always suffer losses. Therefore, sometimes they want right and wrong, and sometimes they do not.

Jingjie Gong (Tao Yuanming) has a poem that says, "Glory and decline are not fixed, but shared between us." Can "right" belong exclusively to me? Can "wrong" always belong to others?

Right and wrong are like chastity. Once they are waved away, how can they be summoned back at will?

Lu Zhengxiang's Concern for the Motherland 113

— Ruogu

Former Prime Minister Lu Zhengxiang was a pioneer in China's diplomatic circles. Diplomats Gu Weijun, Wang Zhengting, Wu Chaoshu, Chen Youren, and Shi Zhaoji were all his disciples. When he was stationed in Belgium in his later years, he lost his wife and joined the Benedictine Order of the Catholic Church as a monk. This spring, he will be promoted to the priesthood. Although Lu resides overseas, he is concerned about his motherland. Recently, in view of the difficult national situation and thorny diplomatic issues, he wrote to the Pope in Rome, appealing for blessings on China. He also prays for China three times a day, morning, noon, and evening, in the church. His letters to the country all have specially made postal stamp-style seals, printed with the words "Millions of Hearts, Do Not Forget National Humiliation." This shows a glimpse of Lu's patriotic enthusiasm. Last winter, Lu wrote to the 93-year-old Ma Xiangbo. The original text is recorded as follows: "Joseph, my teacher, is by my side. I received your handwritten letter last month. Reading it, I was overjoyed and could not sleep. It proves that your health has recovered, which is a great joy. I deeply regret that the national situation is difficult, more so than today. The suffering of the people is also greater than today. Although Xiang resides in a monastery, he must cherish his motherland. Recalling the teachings of my late teacher Xu Wensu, looking around at colleagues at home and abroad, the thorniness of handling affairs, coupled with the danger of the world's encirclement, Xiang enters the hall three times a day, morning, noon, and evening, to sincerely pray for the motherland, for colleagues, and for ancestors. I am especially worried that this is not enough. Therefore, I respectfully write to the Roman See, appealing for a special blessing on all my diplomatic colleagues to show love and encouragement. I offer my meager sincerity as a permanent commemoration and strive to complete the legacy of my late teacher Xu Wensu. In addition to sending a copy of the original letter to my former colleagues Gu, Wang, Wu, Chen (Youren), Shi, Wei (Note Dong), and Wang (Jiafu), I have sent a French copy to Envoy Fu. Please present it to you for your perusal, to earn a smile. Respectfully, I wish you peace. Your disciple Lu Zhengxiang, respectfully, 20th year, 12th month, 18th day."

World Small Chronicle 114

— Haike

A 103-Year-Old Long-Lived Person: There is a 103-year-old long-lived person in England, named Alfred Arnold. He has even forgotten that he is so old and has begun working in the film industry. Recently, a film company was producing a film in Elstree, and he enthusiastically participated, serving as an actor. He claims that he will work hard in the future and will definitely become a star. He was born in Bloomsbury in 1828. He is now a full 104 years old. However, looking at his appearance, he seems to be about 70 years old. No one can tell that he is over 100 years old. And his agility and vitality make it seem like he is not even 70 years old. He usually takes long walks or boats on the Serpentine, which keeps him light on his feet. He also said, "When I was in the East, I learned a kind of meditation from India. I still do it to this day, so it keeps me alive and young."

Recording Two Maps of the Brutal Sun's Invasion of Manchuria and Mongolia 115

— Cailiang

Alas, since the Shenyang Incident, more than four months have passed. Alarming news has been heard frequently, and my heart is broken. Yesterday happened to be a holiday, so I invited several comrades to take a trip to the suburbs together to relieve my boredom. On the way back, we passed the Yousheng Travel Agency on Labor Hall Road in this city and went in together for a short rest. As soon as we sat down, we saw two brightly colored maps hanging on the walls of the agency. I was quite surprised and asked about them. Only then did I learn that they were important maps published by the brutal Sun several years ago after surveying various parts of our Northeast. One is called "Outline Map of Manchuria and Korea," and the other is called "New Map of Manchuria and Mongolia." Although their names are different, their content is the same. They are all aimed at invading the entire Manchuria and Mongolia, that is, Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, Rehe, and Eastern Mongolia. Regarding transportation, in addition to our country's inherent railways, they also focus on the recently completed Jihui Road and the north-south South Manchuria Railway as the main lines. For all important towns along the line that can connect to the hinterland, the distance and how to get there are analyzed in detail. What is especially noteworthy is that the names of all small markets are marked in Japanese. Their ambition for invasion is clearly visible. In addition, famous products of the Eastern Provinces, such as soybeans, wool, coal, iron, and wood, are drawn in detail in the locations of each production area. They are all lifelike and full of tempting colors. Furthermore, each port where Japanese consuls are stationed must have a sun flag drawn as a symbol. Now that I have seen this map today, I feel even more heartache. I still remember hearing Mr. Huang Ren's words when he returned from Japan last spring: when he was traveling in Fusang, he often saw a new map of Manchuria and Mongolia hanging on the desks of large and small agencies in that country. And on the billboards of various stations, the words "Go to Manchuria and Mongolia" were often seen. That country's plot against us is so urgent. What will we do? I know that sitting and talking is far less effective than getting up and acting quickly. After I finished looking at this map, I couldn't help but sigh. Then I thought that some of my compatriots may not fully know about it, so I picked up my pen to record it.

A Bird Catcher's Words 116

— Jingmengdie

Wujin has a 　lake. The area west of the lake is rich in yellow finches. Their taste is delicious, surpassing even pigeon meat. They can be served with wine and can be used as a side dish. It is a famous local product of this village. They are often taken as gifts for relatives and friends. Therefore, residents of the lakeside catch them and sell them in the market for money, no less than a sideline for fishermen. This autumn, there are more fish and crabs, and yellow finches are also particularly abundant. Although the price is not high, the income of bird catchers is naturally abundant.

Yellow finches mostly live on reed beaches, like geese who like to live by the water and flock together. Bird catchers do not divine the day but the night. The most suitable nights are those with a faint moon and a light breeze. The vision of finches at night is dull, but their hearing is sharp. If a strong wind shakes the reeds, the finches will settle down and stop flying, making it difficult for people to start. If the night is still and there is no wind, then the quiet footsteps of people are easily detected. They avoid disaster and fly away. Only when the breeze sways and the reeds rustle, mixing with our quiet footsteps, will the finches not be aware. They seem like wooden 　.

Northern Tour Images and Others (2) 117

— Yao Sufeng

A Self-Narration by Movie Star Hu Die

To put it more deeply, women in our country often suffer from social oppression and bullying; under widespread oppression and bullying, the weak succumb, while the strong continue to struggle. However, we must know that the methods of struggle may be different, but the strength of struggle is the same. Why does society value female dignitaries on the political stage too much, while undervaluing female actresses in the artistic realm?

I dare say that if this distorted social psychology does not change, then no art, no women's movement can have any hope of success.

The conversation is getting farther and farther away. The motive for writing this article is to faithfully expose the life of a professional woman who is noticed by many people. I am not doing a stereotypical eulogy for Ms. Hu Die, nor am I doing free publicity for Ms. Hu Die or the films she stars in. Here, I hope people will know some of the true artistic life of movie actresses, not as people usually guess.

| The following are all the words of Ms. Hu Die, which I have faithfully recorded. | Sufeng

Ms. Hu Die said

The transition from North Sichuan Road to Dumei Road seems to have a kind of "transition" Shanghai has never given me any interest; what gives me interest is only my family and my work. Therefore, what I call "transition" is a transformation from one aspect of freedom and leisure to many aspects of labor. However, I am not without a deep understanding of my life | indeed, not just my life | due to the increase in experience. I believe that my labor is helping my freedom and leisure; and I also believe that those who do not work may be people without freedom and leisure; therefore, my labor has also become a meaningful enjoyment. However, many people in society do not know this, and many people think that being a relatively high-status movie actress is surrounded by a state of intoxication. Ah! Let me tell a story first

People are allowed to catch them. The method is to weave a net into a cover. Cover it from behind. Capture them one by one. Do not startle the others when capturing. If one finch is startled, the flock will fly away. You will not get anything all night. Therefore, those whose experience is not refined and whose skills are not agile do not dare to try it. The loss of one person affects the benefits of others. It will incur public anger and be subject to condemnation and blame. Alas! Catching cicadas and juggling balls each has its own wonders. Even in the smallest of matters in the world, there must be cultivation over time, and there is no chance of good fortune overnight. How much more so in the matter of writing? It is truly as Taishi Gong (Sima Qian) said, "It is difficult to explain to those with shallow views and little knowledge without a love of learning and deep thought, and knowing the reason." Why do junior scholars who have never experienced hardship rashly take up a pen and want to be like Ya Guan Qu Yuan and Xi Wei Ji Shu scolding people? Their intelligence is no greater than that of a fisherman or a bird catcher.

They have received much praise. The exhibition closed the night before.

戎馬雙樓記 119

— 求幸福齋主人

Second Episode: Conversing and Laughing, He Receives Bad News from a Good Teacher; At Home, He Encounters Robbery and Pities His Beloved Friend in Isolation, A Spring-like Atmosphere Arises in the Room. But then I remembered my cousin, An Da Kui. He opened a Fu Ju Xiang silk and satin store in Tianjin. I heard that my father also had some shares in it. In the past, my tuition fees were often remitted from there. The day before yesterday, I wrote to this cousin, asking him to arrange a sum of money to be sent to me first. After the money arrives, I will decide what to do. I am very grateful for your concern. But I can only tell you these things for now. As for what happens in the future, I will talk to you in detail when the time comes. Since we are so close, I will not do anything behind your back. Liang Xiao Yun replied very affectionately. A gentleman bides his time for three years to take revenge. I always advise you not to be too impatient. It's better to study hard in Beijing and talk about it after you graduate. Since the family is already in such a mess, there is no use in you going back. There is even no need to risk that danger. It's not a difficult thing if you only need a few more dollars to spend. Even I, as your friend, can easily help you out. You don't have to write a letter to your uncle asking for it. An Yu Tian couldn't help but smile bitterly. How can I have the nerve to ask you to help me? But you are really too kind to me. I really don't know how to thank you. Liang Xiao Yun suddenly acted coquettishly. I don't come. Other people are sincere and earnest to you, but you always treat me like an outsider. Why are you embarrassed to ask me to help you? And why do you have to say such polite words to thank me? Do you really think I am not worthy of being your friend? An Yu Tian didn't expect that a word would anger this affectionate beauty, so he had to apologize and say, "Okay, okay. It's my fault for being muddled and not knowing how to speak. Please don't be angry. Don't blame me. Now that I am so lonely and isolated, I really need friends to help me. What's more, you are such a good friend. I can't ask for anything more. I'm just afraid that I'm not worthy. How dare I be so ungrateful and reject you?" Liang Xiao Yun smiled slightly.

"Okay, that's settled. I'm determined to be your friend. And I'm not afraid that you'll dislike me. Anyway, you won't be so embarrassed to say you dislike me to my face, right? Now is the time when you are sad. I won't argue with you anymore. Let me do my best to accompany you and coax you. Otherwise, you'll be bored to death. Look, the room is so cold and icy. You've been crying and weeping here alone for so many days. What are you doing? Why are you torturing yourself like this? There's no one else here today. I'm sure you haven't had a comfortable meal yet. I'll ask the waiter to order some dishes from the restaurant and I'll eat with you." An Yu Tian wanted to stop her, but Liang Xiao Yun was as light as a swallow and had already gone to ask the waiter to take care of it. After a while, the wine and dishes were delivered. They were all very exquisite and delicious foods. Liang Xiao Yun dragged An Yu Tian to his seat and sat beside him. First, she raised the pot in her red sleeve and diligently offered wine. Then she used a spoon to serve food and urged him to eat more. An Yu Tian couldn't refuse and had to eat some. Liang Xiao Yun also talked and laughed cheerfully, picking out some interesting and witty jokes to tell. She never mentioned An Yu Tian's unfortunate family affairs again, trying to dispel An Yu Tian's worries and immerse him in the gentle land of this beautiful scenery. Sure enough, the humble room became spring-like, and a trace of a smile gradually appeared on An Yu Tian's furrowed brow. Seeing that they were full of wine and food, the waiter suddenly came in to report, "Mr. An, there's a phone call. It's from the Normal University. It's someone named Li. Please answer it quickly." An Yu Tian couldn't help but be shocked. He pushed his cup away and got up, hurrying away. If you want to know what happened, please wait for the next episode.

The Market for Dried Lily Flowers (Golden Needles) in North-South Goods Softens 131

Last week, the price of dried lily flowers rose slightly (by one or two taels for high-grade goods) due to strong demand from buyers from Guangdong province. However, observing recent market trends, it seems that the appetites of these buyers have been satisfied. Consequently, the previously firm market has softened. Furthermore, dealers from Fujian province also seem eager to sell, indicating a possible decline in prices in the future, especially for lower-grade goods, such as those with a darker color. It is unlikely that these goods will see favorable prices again before the year-end settlement.

Exceedingly Low Price for Raw White Silk in New York 132

Only equivalent to 720 taels of Chinese silver per 100 catties.

Yesterday, the silk market in this port became increasingly sluggish. According to reports, silk sales in the New York market continued to be weak. The telegraph price for Shanghai raw white silk, grade B, was only $1.70 USD per pound, equivalent to only 720 taels of Chinese silver per 100 catties. Factories must lose over 400 taels per bale, making it increasingly difficult to sell. The demand for coarse English and French yellow and white silks was also low, and the market was quiet with little trading reported.

Special Chunmee Tea Transactions Continue to be Strong 133

Yesterday, in the tea market of this port, foreign firms competed with Xiehe, Jinjiang, Baochang, and other companies to actively seek out and purchase special Chunmee tea from the inland producing regions. The total transaction volume reached over 400 boxes. The top-grade Tunxi tea from renowned producers opened at 142 taels, and the market price remained unchanged from the previous day. However, several trading firms have been sending out large numbers of telegrams in recent days, indicating a potential increase in market activity. There have also been sporadic transactions of our Chunmee and Showmee teas reported.

The Trend of Metals and White Lead Sheets is Weak and Weary 134

Due to the closure of various businesses, the metal market has been showing a sluggish trend in recent days. Although white lead sheets had a brief period of growth, the current trend is also very cold. Moreover, those holding existing goods are eager to sell them off quickly, so the future of the standard goods is increasingly bleak. Currently, #2 is priced at 24.5 taels, #3 at 26 taels, #4 at 25 taels, #5 at 22 taels, #6 at 21.5 taels, #7 at 21 taels, #8 at 22.5 taels, and #9 and #10 are both estimated at 20 taels. As for the thick, patterned ones, they are only priced at 18 or 19 taels. This is not in line with the previous standard, according to reports.
