China Reclamation Bank Builds a Mansion 149

Zhao Xintai Construction Company Wins the Bid

Construction Cost 382,000 Taels of Silver

The China Reclamation Bank was founded by Qin Runqing, Wang Boyuan, Xu Jiying, Li Fushun, Zhou Zongliang, Liang Chenlan, and other giants of the financial industry in this city. It collected a full capital of 2.5 million silver dollars in one go. Since its establishment, it has been three years, and its business has become increasingly developed, so that the old buildings on Ningbo Road feel cramped and insufficient for office use. Therefore, the Board of Directors decided to purchase a base of one mu and three fen at the corner of Beijing Road and Jiangxi Road, valued at 250,000 taels of silver. Tonghe Foreign Company designed and built an eight-story mansion. Bids were invited at the end of last year. As a result, Zhao Xintai Construction Company won the bid with a construction cost of 382,000 taels of silver. At present, the project has started. The bank plans to reserve the ground floor and the first and second floors for its own use. All equipment will be extensively adopted from the latest Chinese and foreign bank buildings to ensure that both itself and customers feel comfortable and convenient. The remaining floors will be rented out as office space, and so on.

A Clever Thief in Western Shanghai 150

Breaks Glass Windows Silently

Has Stolen Before and After More Than Ten Times

The North China Daily News reports that in the past thirty days, a clever thief, or perhaps several accomplices, has been stealing from the front and back of foreign residences in the western district more than ten times. The total loss of each owner is estimated to be as high as 15,000 yuan. Once, a German's leather coat was stolen, which was said to be worth more than 6,000 yuan. On Tuesday morning, the thief stole clothes worth 100 yuan from No. 1, Da Xiqu. The thief steals by breaking glass windows to enter people's homes. His technique is very clever, so that people in the house do not hear the sound. The Western District Police Station investigated the stolen households and saw that the thief's entry methods were the same, so they dared to conclude that it was done by one person. After many days of investigation, there are now some clues, and it is expected that the thief can be arrested within a few days.

The Bandit Who Injured the Car Exhibitor Seriously Was Sentenced After Recovery 151

Sentenced to Three Years and Six Months in Prison

Liu Yunsheng, 33 years old, a former coachman living at No. 23 Jin Yi Lane, Beile Road, French Concession, learned on the morning of October 27 last year that Qiu Songlin had more than 1,000 yuan in cash in Liangqinfang, Lafayette Road, and was transporting it to a certain place. He immediately gathered three or four accomplices to hold weapons and wait at the entrance of Liangqinfang. Seeing Qiu ordering people to lift the silver box onto the car, they rushed forward to rob it. Fortunately, the coachman saw the opportunity and drove forward at full speed, and was not robbed. At that time, the police whistle sounded and the accomplices fled without a trace. However, Liu had jumped onto the car's running board. Because the car was driving fast, he was shocked and lost his footing. He fell at the intersection of Lafayette Road and Xiai Road and was injured. His abdomen ruptured and his intestines flowed out. The police brought Liu into the police station and transferred him to Renji Hospital for treatment. At the same time, the victim reported the situation to the police station and asked for an investigation. The details were recorded in previous reports. By December 30, Liu had recovered from his illness and was brought back to the police station by the detective and sent to the Second Special Court. He was prosecuted for attempted robbery under Article 348 of the Criminal Law. Judge Luo Renji opened the court for questioning many times. The victim had left Shanghai and did not arrive. When questioning the defendant, he denied gathering accomplices to rob and claimed that he was injured by the car. According to the victim's bodyguard and the doorman of Liangqinfang, they arrived to testify that they had witnessed the defendant jumping on the car. The defendant hired a lawyer to defend him. The court ordered the trial to be concluded and scheduled a sentencing date. Yesterday was the sentencing date. At 10:00 AM, Judge Luo attended the Criminal Division 1 court and ordered the defendant to be brought to court. Liu Yunsheng was sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment for the crime of attempted robbery by ganging up with three or more people.

Su Gengsheng Hanged Himself in Prison 153

A Cloth Belt Ended a Life

In Xilao, Huade Road, there was a prisoner named Su Gengsheng, a native of Jiangbei, 26 years old, who was sentenced to two years and six months of imprisonment by the court on October 20, 1930, for the crime of theft. Su suddenly strangled himself with a cloth belt in Xilao at around 7:00 AM the day before yesterday. Chinese Constable No. 3, who was in charge of the prison, found it and tried to take him down, but he had already died. The body was carried to the Feilun Road Examination Office. Yesterday morning, Guo Huaipu, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, came to the office to examine and clarify the case. According to the Chinese Constable's report on the situation at that time, Mr. Guo then instructed the examination to find that the deceased prisoner Su Gengsheng had indeed died by hanging himself before his death. The corpse was collected by the corpse uncle Su Yingting for coffin burial.

The Abducted Wealthy Widow Has Escaped Danger 154

Came to Court Yesterday to Prove Everything

On the night of the 10th of this month, the home of Wang Yu, a resident of 71 Tai'an Lane, North Shanxi Road, was robbed by bandits, who sent a letter demanding a huge ransom. They also agreed to meet at the entrance of the Anle Palace Hotel on Edouard Road at 8:30 the night before yesterday to negotiate. The Huishi Police Station learned of this and sent detectives to arrest them, resulting in a shootout. As a result, two bandits, Xiao Wang and Li, were shot and killed on the spot. Jiang Dinghui, a native of Shaoxing, was captured. The bodies of the two bandits were carried to the Feilun Road Examination Office. Yesterday morning, Guo Huaipu, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, came to the office to examine and clarify the case. According to Wang Yu, her husband had passed away and was previously engaged in the gold business. The two dead bandits were indeed the people who kidnapped me. Then, Chinese and Western detectives reported the course of the armed fight at that time. Mr. Guo verified the confession and then instructed the examination to find that the two dead bandits had indeed been shot dead by the detectives before their death. The corpses were coffined by Pushan Villa. After the detectives and the bandits fought, the bandits knew that the matter was defeated and the arrest was very tight, so they released the hostage Wang Yu and sent her home at 9:00 PM the night before yesterday, so she was able to come out and testify today. At midnight last night, Chinese Detective Feng Baishun and Detective Yan Wu continued to arrest two suspects, Wang Xianqiao and Zhang Maoxi, in Room 20, Qixin Hotel, Fuzhou Road. They were taken back to the police station for questioning. They denied being bandits and sued the police chief, who ordered them to be detained for investigation.

The Remarkable Effectiveness of Medicinal Wine for Treating Painful Gout 156

Gout is a condition caused by deficiency of qi and blood, excessive mental strain, weakened spirit, and the invasion of wind and dampness into the bones. This leads to symptoms such as sore bones, numbness in the limbs, hemiplegia, and difficulty walking. If left untreated, it can spread, causing wind and dampness to penetrate the bones, posing a threat to life. Now, the Xiong Biao Brand medicinal wine for treating painful gout, invented by the Xiaoxiantang Pharmacy in Fushoufang, outside the South City Xiaoximen, specializes in treating both new and chronic gout, sore limbs, numb hands and feet, and hemiplegia. Regular consumption can transform weakness into strength. Furthermore, if the medicinal wine is heated and rubbed on the affected area, its effect is miraculous, it is said.

Letter to the Editor 161

To the Editor,

Having read in yesterday's newspaper about the preparatory committee of the Shenxin No. 6 Cotton Mill holding a meeting, with Wu Xiaozhi as chairman, we would like to clarify that the workers of our mill, feeling the need to organize a trade union, previously elected several representatives to hold a preparatory meeting at the Hudong District Cotton Mill Union in the Shezhuang Temple of the Wang Family Residence, west of Gao Laobridge. There were no other organizations or activities. As for Mr. Wu, he is not a worker of our mill. How could he lead the workers of our mill to organize? We hope you will publish this letter in the letter column to clarify the truth and avoid confusing the public.

Sincerely,

The Preparatory Committee of the Shenxin No. 6 Cotton Mill

To the Editor,

Having read in today's newspaper's local news column the "Declaration of the Federation of Trade Unions," which included the name of the Municipal Pharmaceutical Workers' Union, we would like to clarify that in this city, the only pharmaceutical workers' organization is our "Shanghai Pharmaceutical Vocational Union." There is no other trade union under that name. However, our union did not send representatives to participate in the Federation of Trade Unions, nor did we receive any notification. Fearing that this may cause confusion among the public, we have specially prepared this letter for correction. We request that it be published in the letter column. Thank you.

Sincerely,

Shanghai Pharmaceutical Vocational Union, January 20th.

To the Editor,

Having read yesterday's local news in your newspaper regarding the news item of (Zhang Xilin Kidnapping Case, Four Bandits Sentenced to Death), it mentions the lawyer of the police station, Ru Bao Yi, stating that although the defendant Wang Xingcun was declared not guilty, in the self-accusation of the encroachment case, "it was the Anhui Fellow Association who accused him" and that he was sentenced to four months in prison. We are extremely surprised. Wang Xingcun is a member of our association. Last October, he was mistakenly detained by the police station. We sent a letter to the Shanghai First Special District Court to prove that Wang was a kind and law-abiding fellow villager who was falsely accused. We requested a fair trial and release. At the same time, we also proved that other fellow villagers who were mistakenly detained in the same case had been released. All are on record. There is no reason to accuse Wang Xingcun. The report is misleading and we request a correction. Thank you.

Sincerely,

Anhui Fellow Association in Shanghai, January 20th.

Reader Correspondence

Answers Regarding Student Work 162

— Fan Hansheng

Since the national crisis occurred, most of the people across the country have been living in anger, depression, resentment, and confusion, especially the young students who are most rich in emotion. They resent the brutality of Japanese imperialism and the incompetence of the League of Nations, but they resent even more the military non-resistance and diplomatic helplessness of the government authorities that maintain two million soldiers. However, in utter disappointment, they once enthusiastically went to various places to promote their cause, they once lingered on the streets to raise donations, they once organized volunteer armies, they once endured hunger and cold to petition the government in the capital, and they once engaged in "venting" work such as marches, demonstrations, posting slogans, and shouting slogans. Finally, they painfully went on strike, wanting to awaken the government, but in fact, the facts tell us that in the past three or four months, they not only failed to achieve the goal of saving the country, but also sacrificed a lot of precious time, earned a tired heart, and fell into a path of disappointment and negativity. We know that the young students of the May Fourth and May Eighth Movements are now the people in charge in politics and society. Their patriotic enthusiasm and determination to save the country at that time were no less than those of the average young student today. However, because they refused to enrich their own learning and refused to do practical work, when they took office, they were the same as the people they hated before, and were hated by others, resulting in the current situation of internal and external troubles. Therefore, in the future, we should no longer follow the same path as before. I think what young students should strive for now is not to petition the government or declare war on Japan, nor to engage in bare-handed military training. The most practical work is to "go deep into the people to awaken the masses and organize the masses," because if national affairs rely only on the ruling class and the intellectual class, it is absolutely impossible. Unless four hundred million idiots take responsibility, China will never be strong. This great and meaningful work can only be done by young students, and only young students are willing to do it. Therefore, young students should not be afraid of difficulties and do this work to make it happen as soon as possible. I dare to guarantee that "if four hundred million idiots are awakened, their amazing power will surely shake the world and make the imperialists pale in fright."

In addition to doing this work, we should also enrich our own knowledge, because to maintain a great nation in the world, to build a strong country, we must have sufficient academic preparation. The reason why Japan is so strong is also the result of their efforts in academics in the last fifty or sixty years. It is better to say that Japan occupied our Northeast with academics than to say that they occupied our Northeast with military force this time. Bacon of England said, "Knowledge is power." This is not a bad word. Looking at the world today, no matter what powerful tools are manufactured and used in wartime or peacetime, none of them are not related to the level of knowledge. Therefore, improving knowledge is a permanent work of resisting insults. In the future, we should strive towards this goal. Overthrowing imperialism cannot be achieved by temporary emotions. Noisy shouts and aimless wandering will only disappoint us. We have the spirit of "swallowing blood and teeth" as Zeng Guofan said, and with a twelve-point serious sense of responsibility, we firmly and vigorously recognize the goal and strive forward. We will eventually have a day of victory. (B)

Shenbao Local Supplement 164

Small Forum

Lucky New Route 165

According to yesterday's newspaper, the Yangtze River route has been obstructed since October last year. The water is shallow and the shoals are high, and large ships of 5,000 tons or more cannot sail. Therefore, large ships have been suspended for several months. As a result of careful and precise measurements by customs officials, a new route was discovered with 15 feet of deep water that can be navigated without obstruction. Reading this news made me have a little thought.

The National Government is like the engine room of a ship, the government authorities are like the engineers on the ship, and we ordinary people are like the passengers on the ship. We only know that we want to go to our destination. Our destination is to live and work in peace, without being infringed upon by other countries from the outside, and without being persecuted by hunger and calamity from the inside. This is the only hope of the ordinary people for the government. It is like the passengers on the ship hoping that the engineers will not go the wrong route, so that the ship sinks and people drown.

But at present, we seem to feel that the route taken by the engineers on our ship is not quite correct. Perhaps it is even the wrong route. At first, we thought it was just a matter of detouring a few miles and spending a little more travel time. We still tried our best to endure it, but the situation has worsened recently. It bumped on this reef and ran aground on that shoal. The ship's body is already a little unstable. Who knew that a hurricane and storm one night, a big hole was pierced in the northeast corner of our ship's body. The terrible Eastern Ocean tide just kept rushing in. The lives of our passengers are really in extreme danger. Aren't our engineers going to give us a quick full power and correct the route?

If there is still a new route to be found on a Yangtze River, is it possible that there is no new route to be found in China in the vast Pacific Ocean? May our government immediately correct the route and re-establish the policy of saving the country and the people, and stop bumping into reefs and running around on shoals!

Popular Literature and Art

The Attic Class 166

— Ding Nu

We know that since the imperialists brought their economic aggression that kills without bloodshed and issued the general attack order, China's society, economy, and politics have been bombed to pieces. We have seen with our own eyes that the rural economy has collapsed suddenly, and batches of vagrants have gone to the cities to concentrate. Later, China's politics could not get on the right track, and economic problems could not be solved. The number of unemployed people increased day by day, and the world's depression further sharpened it. As a result, the attic class was established.

In recent years, I have personally seen many friends. Since they stepped out of the school gate, they ran around everywhere and had no way out. In the end, they had no choice but to become members of the attic class. Even some of them bathed in the sea of people for a while, and because they were not used to the stinky air, they retreated to this last line of defense like defeated soldiers. Therefore, now, no matter where you go in Shanghai, north of Shanghai, east of Shanghai, or west of Shanghai, we can find the shadow of the attic, and these attics are mostly full.

People who live in attics are not all literary beggars. Many of them are idle after eating their fill, waiting for opportunities. Most of them are greedy for cheapness. As long as they pay a few dollars a month, one of the three major problems in life is solved. During the day, if they are happy, they may as well do it themselves, or go to a nearby restaurant. Otherwise, three sesame cakes for a meal is nothing. Although life is hard, it has never been lost in dullness; although the enjoyment of material trade is a little worse, the spirit is happy.

In the past, the attic was once used by proletarian writers, who were enthusiastically shouting the slogan "The workers and peasants rise up." Although the power is not so great now, we believe that many masterpieces have been drafted in the attic. Therefore, the attic class seen in academics is more meaningful than the attic class seen in ordinary times.

People who live in the attic can be said to be extremely comfortable. No matter how fierce the artillery fire is outside and the killing sounds are everywhere, the attic will not be destroyed by it. Therefore, the existence of the attic class is a very good phenomenon.

From the above discussion, we recognize that the attic is a microcosm of China's economic situation, which is absolutely true. The characters of the attic class can be regarded as examples of the bankruptcy of modern education, and finally, what makes these characters have no way out is, of course, that politics is not on the right track, industry is not prosperous, and there are all kinds of diseases. Therefore, I say that the attic can really be said to be a microcosm of the current situation in China!

Popular Science

How to Get Clean Water to Drink 169

— Tao Xiaotao

If we want clean water, there are two ways: 1) Distillation. 2) Filtration. I will write them separately below...

1) Distillation

Take a flask, put five-thirds of water in the middle, and plug the mouth of the flask with a soft cork. Insert a curved glass tube in the middle of the cork. Then insert the short end of the tube into the flask, but do not reach the water surface, and extend the longer end out of the flask. Then put a section of bamboo tube on the longer end of the glass tube, and let cold water flow in the bamboo tube. Then put an empty bottle at the lower end of the glass tube and put the empty bottle in cold water. Then use fire to burn under the flask. When the water boils, the steam will escape from the glass tube, and when it meets the cold in the bamboo tube, the steam will turn into water and run from the tube into the bottle. This water is distilled water. It is necessary to change the cold water in the bamboo tube frequently to prevent it from getting hot and preventing the steam from condensing into water. This distilled water is very hygienic. Chemical reagents and hospitals use this distilled water. It takes one or two hours to distill a small cup of distilled water in the laboratory. A large amount of distilled water must be handled by the factory.

2) Filtration

Take a flower pot, and put a piece of sponge in the hole at the bottom of the flower pot (if there is no sponge, you can use loofah). Then spread a layer of charcoal chips more than an inch thick on the bottom of the pot; spread a layer of clean fine sand on the charcoal chips; and spread a layer of coarse gravel two inches thick on the fine sand. This water filter is successful. Pour the dirty water into the flower pot, and in a moment, clean water will flow out of the small hole at the bottom of the pot. It is better to boil the filtered water before drinking. The water filter should also be washed frequently to avoid unclean things remaining inside. This flower pot water filter is very practical, and it only costs three cents to make it.

Street Sociology

Various Ways of Living (5) 170

— Xingzi

If you want to watch a play, you don't have to spend money to go to the big stage, Tianchan Stage and other big theaters. There are plenty of them on the New World, the Great World, and all other relatively wide roads, and the plays here are not only cheap, but also have a special charm that is enough for you to savor. If you don't have any money with you, you can listen to a song for free and slip away.

The signboards of this theater are often open-air stage, free stage, solo stage, small stage, and people's stage. These terms are very appropriate, and open-air and free vividly depict its entire pattern. Of course, none of the audience is a rich man or a VIP, nor is there a fashionable lady or young master. Naming it the people's stage is also just right.

Most of these stages only have three or two roles, and some only have one person, which is the solo stage.

A beautiful "king" or "official" crown made of red and green paper is crookedly worn on a head covered with powder, painted with ink, and with messy hair. He is also draped in a dirty and unbearable broken opera costume, pacing slowly, with "dang, dang, dang, dang, Zong" in his mouth. Another person leisurely pulls the erhu, and the curtain of the play opens here. If he sings the play "Baochan Offering Wine" or "The Heavenly Maiden Scattering Flowers," the grotesque appearance of twisting and turning and the broken voice will really make you laugh or cry.

They mostly have to take on several roles by themselves, and the gong, drums, erhu, and all other instruments are also concurrently played by one mouth. They have no fixed location. Wherever they go, they perform.

After a play is finished, it is customary to say, "Friends, please help," "If you don't have money, please help with the applause." Three or five coins, you can give as much as you want.

Is this playing with life? Or is it playing tricks on life?

East, West, South, North

Although they are persuaded horizontally to work diligently despite their illness, and persuaded vertically to come out of the mountains again, the persuaders are earnest, but the listeners are dismissive. As a result, the general audience is really tired of watching... Everyone discussed a solution and decided to issue a warning first...

"Adding Officials" has been done for many days,

The main character has not appeared on stage...

The medicine has been changed, but the soup has not,

Who cares that the black mountains and white waters are full of smoke?

In this turbulent and tense situation, there is a main character who is leisurely living his life of extreme happiness! What kind of extreme happiness is it? Listen to me sing!

Shanghai Stories

Shanghai Stories (15) 172

— Compiled and Translated by Zhou Rong

Xiao Dao Hui Occupies Shanghai III - The Origin of Xiao Dao Hui

In 1851 (the first year of Xianfeng), after the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom army was launched from Guangdong and Guangxi, it spread to the Yangtze River basin. At the same time, Xiao Dao Hui, a branch of the Sanhehui, began to operate and occupied Xiamen. The Xiao Dao Hui worshipped Taoism and allowed smoking opium. Since their religious beliefs were different from those of the Taiping Army, they were despised by the Taiping Army.

On September 7th of the third year of Xianfeng, a part of the Xiao Dao Hui sneaked into Shanghai and soon occupied Shanghai City. That day happened to be the day of the autumn sacrifice to the Confucius Temple. The city gates were wide open, and 600 members of the Xiao Dao Hui followed the crowd into the city and attacked various government offices. Magistrate Yuan Zude was killed, and Wu Jianzhang, the governor of Songhu Tai, was trapped in his private residence. At that time, the insiders in the city threw red cloth on the streets. The members of the Xiao Dao Hui took the red cloth on their heads, so they were called "red heads." The leader of the Xiao Dao Hui was Liu Lichuan, a native of Guangdong, who was originally a sugar merchant. He had organized the Sanhehui in Shanghai a few years ago. Liu Lichuan was addicted to opium, but he was quite capable and decisive. His subordinate, Chen Alin, had some talent and directed the operations in the middle. He was actually the leader of the Xiao Dao Hui. The Xiao Dao Hui's purpose of overthrowing the Manchu government and calling on the people was originally no different from the Taiping Army's doctrine of revitalizing the Han and destroying the Manchus. The official books of the time called this rebellion the rebellion of the Min-Guang Hui bandits, but the general public called it the rebellion of Xiaojinzhu, because Xiaojinzhu was Liu Lichuan's nickname.

After the city fell, the Xiao Dao Hui had internal strife and divided into the Guangdong gang and the Fujian gang. The Guangdong gang accused the Fujian gang of looting too much, and the order became chaotic.

At that time, Wu Jianzhang, the governor of Songhu Tai, was still trapped in his private residence. Two foreigners, one Dr. Hale and one Mr. Smith, sneaked into the city from the concession, went to Wu Jianzhang's private residence, disguised him, and escaped from the city at night. First, they went to the home of missionary Dr. Anmata, because the doctor's house was near the city wall, and then moved to Qichang Foreign Company. Wu Jianzhang was thus spared.
